**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Entrance pupil position + size** (OPTICS-ENTRANCE-PUPIL-POS): paraxial reverse-trace of a marginal ray from the aperture stop through the front sub-stack (Welford 1986 §4.4 / Hecht §6.6); position_z_mm from first surface vertex; D-element transverse magnification; converging front → real pupil (positive z); diverging front → virtual pupil (negative z); LLM tool `optics_compute_entrance_pupil`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; exit pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Exit pupil position + size** (OPTICS-EXIT-PUPIL-POS): paraxial two-ray forward trace from the aperture stop through the rear sub-stack (Welford 1986 §4.4 / Hecht §6.6); position_z_mm from last surface vertex; radius from stop-edge ray height at exit pupil plane; thin-lens identity (stop at last surface → EP at z=0, m=1); BK7 biconvex → virtual exit pupil (z≈−3.41 mm, Welford §4.4 oracle); afocal telescope (f_obj=100 mm, f_eye=25 mm) → Ramsden disk at z=31.25 mm, radius=1.25 mm, m=0.25=1/M_telescope (Hecht §6.6 oracle); LLM tool `optics_compute_exit_pupil`; 43 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; entrance pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Diffraction-limited MTF for circular aperture** (OPTICS-MTF-DIFFRACTION-LIMITED): closed-form on-axis MTF(ν) = (2/π)[arccos(ν/ν₀) − (ν/ν₀)·√(1−(ν/ν₀)²)] for ν ≤ ν₀, 0 otherwise; cutoff ν₀ = 1/(λ·F#) (Goodman "Introduction to Fourier Optics" §6.4 eq. 6-49; Hecht "Optics" 5e §11.3.3); oracle: λ=550nm, F/4 → ν₀=454.5 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0, MTF(ν₀/2)≈0.391 — all validated to < 0.1%; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: diffraction-limited theoretical upper bound only — no aberrations (Seidel S_I–S_V), no defocus, no wavefront error, no sensor MTF; monochromatic only (polychromatic = ∫W(λ)·MTF(λ)dλ, not implemented); on-axis only; circular aperture only.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Pixel aperture MTF + Nyquist limit** (OPTICS-PIXEL-MTF): `PixelSensorSpec(pixel_pitch_um, fill_factor=1.0)` → `PixelMtfReport(nyquist_freq_cyc_per_mm, mtf_curve, mtf_at_nyquist, mtf_at_50_percent_nyquist, honest_caveat)`; pixel aperture MTF = |sinc(π·a·ν)| where a = pitch·fill_factor (Boreman "MTF in Optical and Electro-Optical Systems" §3.4; Hecht §11.3); Nyquist limit ν_N = 1/(2·p) caps detectable spatial frequency; oracle (p=1.5μm, ff=1.0): ν_N=333.33 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0 exactly, MTF(ν_N)=2/π≈0.6366 — all validated to < 1e-6; fill_factor < 1 → narrower aperture → slower sinc roll-off → MTF at Nyquist > 2/π (verified: ff=0.5 → MTF(ν_N)≈0.900); `combine_mtf_curves(optical, pixel)` for incoherent cascade MTF_system = MTF_optical × MTF_pixel (Boreman §2.1); LLM tool `optics_compute_pixel_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: PIXEL APERTURE SINC ONLY — NOT modelled: silicon carrier-diffusion MTF (lateral minority-carrier spread vs. depth, Boreman §3.4); inter-pixel electrical/optical crosstalk; anti-aliasing filter MTF; Bayer CFA demosaicing resolution loss; charge-transfer inefficiency (CCD); non-square pixels; 2-D MTF = product of independent 1-D sincs for square pixel. Ref: Boreman (2001) §3.4, §2.1; Hecht (2017) §11.3; Holst & Lomheim (2007) §5.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/pixel_mtf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Petzval field curvature** (OPTICS-PETZVAL-CURVATURE-COMPUTE): Petzval sum P = Σ (n_after − n_before) / (n_before · n_after · R_i) (Hecht §6.3.2 / Born & Wolf §4.5); Petzval radius R_P = 1/P; flat-field score 1/(1+|P|·100); BK7 biconvex oracle (R1=+50, R2=−50, n=1.5168): P ≈ 0.01363 mm⁻¹, R_P ≈ 73.4 mm (within 1%); flat-field condition Σφ/n = 0 → P = 0 verified; plano surfaces (|R|=1e18) contribute 0; stop-shift invariance; per-surface breakdown with is_plano flag; LLM tool `optics_compute_petzval_curvature`; 26 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial (third-order) only; does NOT include astigmatism (S_III term); P=0 guarantees flat Petzval sphere but not zero field curvature in the presence of astigmatism (Hecht §6.3.2); thick-lens pupil-shift corrections not modelled.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Spot diagram + encircled energy** (OPTICS-SPOT-DIAGRAM): fan-of-rays trace through sequential lens system; ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) × ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) Cartesian pupil grid over unit disk (Welford 1986 §8.2); exact meridional y-intercept via Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect (Welford §5.2-5.3); first-order sagittal x estimate (Hecht §5.7); `SpotDiagramResult` dataclass: image_points_xy (list[(float,float)], mm), rms_radius_mm (Welford §8.2 RMS), encircled_80pct_radius_mm (geometric EE80 radius, Hecht §6.3), centroid_xy, svg_diagram (SVG with RMS/EE80/Airy-disk rings + centroid marker + scale bar), honest_caveat; weak-lens paraxial singlet on-axis → near-zero y-spread; BK7 biconvex singlet at 10° → rms > on-axis (coma verified; Hecht §6.3 / Welford §6); EE80 ≥ RMS monotonically; LLM tool `optics_compute_spot_diagram` (monochromatic only; sagittal x = first-order estimate; no chromatic dispersion; single wavelength; stop at first surface; 24 hermetic tests). Ref: Hecht (2017) §6.3, §10.2; Welford (1986) §5.2-5.3, §6, §8.2.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Piston/tip/tilt/defocus wavefront alignment analysis** (OPTICS-WAVEFRONT-PISTON-TIP-TILT): extracts Z₁ (piston), Z₂ (tip), Z₃ (tilt), Z₄ (defocus) Noll-ordered Zernike alignment components from a sampled wavefront W(ρ,θ); reports each in waves at a given wavelength via W_nm / wavelength_nm conversion; reuses fit_zernike_wavefront (4-term least-squares, numpy.linalg.lstsq, Noll 1976 orthonormal basis); `PistonTipTiltReport` dataclass (piston_waves, tip_waves, tilt_waves, defocus_waves, residual_rms_waves, dominant_misalignment, honest_caveat); dominant = argmax(|c_j|) for j=1..4 with "none" below 0.001 wave threshold; LLM tool `optics_analyze_wavefront_alignment`; 45 hermetic tests (pure piston 10nm @ λ=632.8nm → 0.01580 waves verified; pure tip/tilt/defocus; combined misalignment; higher-order residual; error-path). Honest: circular unit-disk pupil only (ρ ∈ [0,1]; no obscuration or elliptical aperture); alignment analysis only — corrects rigid-body misalignment (piston = axial OPD offset, tip/tilt = wavefront tilt, defocus = longitudinal focus); does NOT correct higher-order aberrations (coma, astigmatism, spherical, etc.); use optics_fit_zernike_wavefront for full 15-term decomposition. Ref: Hecht (2017) §11.3; Born & Wolf (1999) §9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992) Applied Optics and Optical Engineering XI ch.1; Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207.

**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Sagitta arrow chart** (OPTICS-SAGITTA-ARROW-CHART): conic + even-power aspheric surface sagitta z(r) sampled across the clear aperture; standard ISO 10110-12 §6.2 / Welford §3.3 formula z = c·r²/(1+√(1−(1+k)c²r²)) + Σaᵢ·r^(2i+4); SVG chart with horizontal axis = radius (mm), vertical = sagitta (mm), arrow markers at every 5th sample showing local slope dz/dr; `AsphericSurfaceSpec` dataclass (radius_mm, conic_k, aspheric_coeffs, clear_aperture_radius_mm); `SagittaArrowChartResult` (sagitta_samples, max_sagitta_mm, conic_only_sagitta_mm, aspheric_contribution_mm, svg_chart, honest_caveat); sphere R=50 r=10 oracle z≈1.0102 verified < 1e-6; paraboloid k=−1 z=r²/(2R) exact; hemisphere z=R at edge; domain-violation guard (radicand ≥ 0 + fp-epsilon clamp); LLM tool `optics_compute_sagitta_arrow_chart`; 28 hermetic tests. Honest: standard conic + even-power polynomial asphere ONLY; no Zernike / freeform / XY-polynomial / Q-polynomial / off-axis / tilted surface support; arrow markers show dz/dr (slope), not surface normal; ISO 10110-12:2019. Ref: Welford (1986) §3.3; ISO 10110-12:2019.

**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Vignetting fraction check** (OPTICS-VIGNETTING-CHECK): computes the fraction of entrance-pupil area occluded by clear-aperture limits at a given field angle; `LensClearApertureSpec` dataclass (surfaces: list of {clear_aperture_radius_mm, axial_position_mm}); `VignettingReport` dataclass (field_angle_deg, vignetting_pct, limiting_surface_idx, effective_pupil_area_pct, honest_caveat); `compute_vignetting(spec, field_angle_deg, marginal_ray_at_stop_mm=10.0)` — paraxial chief-ray displacement Δ_j = z_j·tan(θ); effective pupil area = exact two-circle intersection area (Weisstein formula) of entrance-pupil disk (radius R) with per-surface CA disk (radius r_j, centred at Δ_j); vignetting_pct = (1 − A_eff/A_full)×100; limiting_surface_idx = argmin of per-surface intersection areas; on-axis (field=0°) → vignetting=0 verified; wide-angle (30°) with tight CA → significant clipping verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting_check`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial chief-ray displacement only (no exact ray trace through glass); circular, rotationally-symmetric CAs only; diffraction-induced vignetting NOT modelled; chromatic pupil walk NOT modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) §3.7; Hecht (2017) §5.7.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Telecentricity check** (OPTICS-TELECENTRICITY): `compute_telecentricity(lens_system_dict, field_height_mm=10.0, focus_shift_mm=0.5)` → `TelecentricityReport(chief_ray_angle_object_deg, chief_ray_angle_image_deg, object_telecentric, image_telecentric, both_telecentric, max_magnification_variation_pct, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray trace via Welford nu-form (`n′u′ = nu − hc(n′−n)`); chief-ray solved by superposition: Ray A (H, 0) + α·Ray B (object-dist, 1) at first surface, α = −h_A_stop/h_B_stop forces h=0 at aperture stop; object-space telecentric ↔ |angle_obj| < 0.5°; image-space telecentric ↔ |angle_img| < 0.5°; magnification variation across ±focus_shift_mm computed from u_last of marginal field ray relative to Lagrange-invariant reference magnification; oracle: single-lens (f=100 mm, stop at front focal plane from 5 m object) → object_telecentric=True, image_telecentric=False; doubly-telecentric relay (two equal lenses, stop at shared focal plane) → both_telecentric=True; LLM tool `optics_compute_telecentricity`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: PARAXIAL (first-order) ONLY — chief ray forced through h=0 at stop surface; aspheric surface terms do not affect first-order angle; stop modelled as thin plane; infinite-conjugate objects approximated by large finite distance; magnification variation uses thin-lens paraxial formula (nu-form). Telecentric threshold: |angle| < 0.5° (conventional machine-vision). Ref: Welford "Aberrations of Optical Systems" (1986) §3, §4.4; Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" §5.4; Hecht "Optics" §6.6. `kerf-cad-core/optics/telecentricity_check.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Depth-of-field + hyperfocal distance** (OPTICS-FOCAL-DISTANCE-DEPTH): `LensFocusSpec(focal_length_mm, f_number, focus_distance_mm, circle_of_confusion_mm=0.03)` → `DepthOfFieldReport(hyperfocal_distance_mm, near_limit_mm, far_limit_mm, depth_of_field_mm, behind_focus_fraction, infinity_focus_at_hyperfocal, honest_caveat)`; standard photographic thin-lens DoF formulae (Greenleaf "Photographic Optics" §3 / Hecht "Optics" §6.4): H = f²/(N·c) + f; D_near = D·(H−f)/(H+D−2f); D_far = D·(H−f)/(H−D) [∞ when D ≥ H]; oracle 50mm f/2.8 @ 5 m c=0.03 mm → H ≈ 29811.9 mm (≈29.81 m); near ≈ 4286 mm; far ≈ 5993 mm; DoF ≈ 1707 mm — all verified to < 0.01%; at focus=H: D_near = H/2 exactly, D_far = ∞ verified; D ≥ H → DoF infinite; larger f/# → wider DoF; LLM tool `optics_compute_depth_of_field`; 25 hermetic tests. Default CoC 0.03 mm = 35mm full-frame standard (Greenleaf §3 / 1/1400 diagonal). HONEST: geometric thin-lens model only — does NOT add diffraction-limited Airy-disk blur to geometric CoC; at small apertures (f/# ≳ f/16 for visible light) Airy disk 1.22·λ·N approaches 0.03 mm CoC, so geometric DoF is slightly optimistic; for combined blur circle use c_eff = sqrt(c_geom² + c_airy²). Ref: Hecht (2017) §6.4; Greenleaf (1950) §3; Kingslake (1978) §4.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Working f-number (finite-conjugate)** (OPTICS-FNO-WORKING): `FnoWorkingSpec(nominal_f_number, magnification)` → `FnoWorkingReport(nominal_f_number, working_f_number, exposure_loss_stops, image_irradiance_factor, honest_caveat)`; thin-lens working f-number formula N_w = N·(1+|m|) (Hecht "Optics" §6.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" §4.5); magnification convention m = −s_i/s_o (negative for real inverted images); oracle f/4 at 1:1 macro (m=−1) → N_w=8.0, loss=2.0 stops exactly; f/2.8 at 1:2 (m=−0.5) → N_w=4.2, loss≈1.17 stops; image irradiance factor = (N/N_w)² = 1/(1+|m|)²; exposure_loss_stops = 2·log₂(1+|m|); m=0 (infinity focus) → N_w=N, loss=0, factor=1.0 (no penalty); absolute value of m used so positive (virtual-image) magnifications are handled; LLM tool `optics_compute_working_fno`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: thin-lens (symmetric-pupil) approximation ONLY — real asymmetric lenses (retrofocus, telephoto, macro with floating elements) have pupil magnification p = D_exit/D_entrance ≠ 1; exact formula N_w = (1/p)·N·(1+|m|/p) (Smith MOE §4.5) can differ by 0.5–1 stop for extreme retrofocus designs; pupil-position measurement requires an aperture-stop trace not in scope here. Ref: Hecht (2017) §6.4; Smith (2008) §4.5; Ray (2002) §2. `kerf-cad-core/optics/fno_working.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Iris (aperture stop) diameter map** (OPTICS-IRIS-DIAMETER-MAP): `IrisMapSpec(lens_system_dict, target_f_number, target_efl_mm=None)` → `IrisDiameterReport(iris_diameter_mm, effective_f_number, efl_mm, surface_clearance_check, clipped, honest_caveat)`; paraxial formula D = EFL/f# (Welford "Aberrations" §3.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" §6); EFL computed via canonical marginal-ray trace (h=1, u=0) or supplied via `target_efl_mm`; marginal ray h=D/2 at stop (u=0) traced forward through surfaces after the stop and backward through a reversed sub-system for surfaces before the stop; per-surface clearance_ratio = CA_radius / |h| (>1 = clears; <1 = clips); clipping flag when h > 0.95 × CA_radius; oracle: EFL=50 mm, f/4 → D=12.5 mm exactly; f/1.4 fast lens → D≈35.7 mm; stop_surface_index configurable; LLM tool `optics_compute_iris_diameter_map`; 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: paraxial (first-order) marginal-ray trace only — aspheric higher-order sag terms ignored; D=EFL/f# is infinity-conjugate formula only (finite-conjugate requires working f-number N_w=N·(1+|m|), Smith MOE §4.5); clear apertures are caller-supplied; production design requires exact skew-ray analysis (Zemax OpticStudio / CODE V / Welford §5). Ref: Welford (1986) §3.4; Smith (2008) §6; Hecht (2017) §6.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/iris_diameter_map.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Airy-disk diffraction-limited PSF** (OPTICS-DIFFRACTION-PSF): `DiffractionPSFSpec(wavelength_nm, aperture_diameter_mm, focal_length_mm)` → `DiffractionPSFReport(airy_disk_radius_um, rayleigh_resolution_um, fwhm_um, psf_profile, honest_caveat)`; radial intensity I(r) = [2·J₁(x)/x]² where x = π·D·r/(λ·f) (Hecht "Optics" 5e §10.2, eq. 10.22; Born & Wolf "Principles of Optics" 7e §8.5.2, eq. 8.41); Airy disk radius r_Airy = 1.22·λ·F# (first zero of J₁, Born & Wolf §8.5.2); Rayleigh resolution criterion Δr = r_Airy (Hecht §10.2.7, eq. 10.28); FWHM ≈ 1.03·λ·F# (Hecht eq. 10.59); uses scipy.special.j1 when available with pure-Python ascending-series fallback (Abramowitz & Stegun §9.1.10); oracle λ=550nm, D=10mm, f=50mm (F#=5): r_Airy=3.355 μm, FWHM=2.833 μm, I(0)=1.0, I(r_Airy)≈0 — all validated to <1e-6; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_psf`; 32 hermetic tests. HONEST: SCALAR DIFFRACTION ONLY — no vector/polarisation effects (Richards-Wolf high-NA integral, Born & Wolf §8.7); circular aperture only (non-circular/annular not modelled); aberration-free (Airy pattern = diffraction-limited ideal; Seidel/Zernike wavefront error → Strehl < 1 not modelled); monochromatic (polychromatic PSF = ∫W(λ)·I(r,λ)dλ not implemented); on-axis and paraxial (NA = D/(2f) ≪ 1 assumed). Ref: Hecht (2017) §10.2; Born & Wolf (1999) §8.5; Goodman (2005) §4.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/diffraction_psf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Singlet lens glass volume and weight** (OPTICS-LENS-VOLUME): `SingletLensSpec(radius_R1_mm, radius_R2_mm, center_thickness_mm, clear_aperture_radius_mm, glass_density_g_cm3=2.51)` → `LensVolumeReport(volume_mm3, weight_g, edge_thickness_mm, sag1_mm, sag2_mm, lens_form, honest_caveat)`; sag h = |R| − √(|R|² − r²) (Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" §13.3 eq. 13.6 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging and Aberrations" §1.2); cap volume V_cap = π·h²·(3|R|−h)/3 (Smith §13.3 eq. 13.7); lens volume V = π·r²·t_c ± V_cap1 ± V_cap2 with sign from Cartesian-sign surface convention (convex → subtract, concave → add); oracle: BK7 plano-convex R1=+100 mm, R2=∞, ct=5 mm, CA_r=12.5 mm, ρ=2.51 g/cm³ → sag1=0.7843 mm, V=2261.6 mm³, weight=5.677 g (analytically verified); biconvex symmetric V = cylinder − 2·cap (both surfaces subtract); biconcave V = cylinder + 2·cap (both surfaces add; edge > center thickness); meniscus R1=+100/R2=+200 classified correctly; lens_form ∈ {biconvex, biconcave, plano_convex, plano_concave, meniscus, plano_plano}; LLM tool `optics_compute_lens_volume`; 35 hermetic tests. HONEST: SPHERICAL SURFACES ONLY — aspheric sag h=Rc·r²/(1+√(1−(1+k)c²r²))+Σ A_i·r^(2i) requires numerical integration (out of scope); no anti-reflection coating thickness (AR layers 100–500 nm, negligible mass); homogeneous density assumed (GRIN / melt-gradient glass differs ≤0.3%, Schott TIE-31 §3); clear_aperture_radius ≠ physical blank radius — blank is always larger, giving higher actual weight. Ref: Smith (2008) §13.3; Mahajan (2011) §1.2; Schott TIE-31 (2023). `kerf-cad-core/optics/lens_volume.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** ✅ — **Paraxial chief-ray height trace** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-HEIGHT): `trace_chief_ray(lens_system_dict, field_angle_deg, stop_surface_idx)` → `ChiefRayHeightReport(per_surface_heights, image_height_mm, magnification, stop_surface_idx, chief_ray_at_stop_mm, object_angle_deg, image_angle_deg, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray (principal ray from off-axis object through stop centre) traced via nu-form superposition (Welford "Aberrations" §3 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging" §2): two auxiliary rays (Ray A: object height H, slope 0; Ray B: height obj_dist, slope 1) solve h_stop=0 → u_obj=−h_A_stop/h_B_stop; oracle: f=50mm plano-convex thin lens, θ=5° → image_height=f·tan(5°)=4.374mm (verified to <1e-3mm); chief-ray height at stop = 0 exactly; image-space telecentric condition (stop at front focal plane → u_img=0) verified; per-surface {surface_idx, ray_height_mm, ray_angle_deg}; LLM tool `optics_trace_chief_ray`; 30 hermetic tests. HONEST: PARAXIAL ONLY — first-order heights differ from exact at large field/fast optics; APERTURE STOP POSITION MUST BE SUPPLIED (no auto-detect); rotationally symmetric systems only; image height = f·tan(θ) (no distortion correction). Ref: Welford (1986) §3, §3.7; Mahajan (2011) §2; Smith (2008) §5. `kerf-cad-core/optics/chief_ray_height.py`.

**Implicit geometry** ✅ — F-rep CSG (union/intersect/subtract/blend/shell) + domain warps (twist/taper/wave) in `kerf_cad_core.frep.csg`.

Data: ICE v3.0, Hammond & Jones, University of Bath, 2019 — NOT Ecoinvent (license-restricted).
**Materials + LCA** ✅ — Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty); EoL circularity (EN 15978 Module D + Ellen MacArthur MCI) ✅.

**Compare matrices** ✅ — feature-matrix YAML for 14 reference CADs: Fusion 360, SolidWorks, Onshape, FreeCAD, Rhino, KiCad, CATIA, Creo, NX, Inventor, AutoCAD, Altium, Revit, Blender — 741 grounded rows total.

**Security hardening** ✅ — `/run-topo` auth gate; NFP `grid_step` clamped; PVT `n_mc` clamped; Yosys module-name injection blocked; shared `_guard_*` helpers extracted across 68 files (−2009/+129 lines net).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-CROSS-CURVE** ✅ — walk a parametric path on the Catmull-Clark subdivision-surface limit and intersect with a planar cut to produce a cross-section curve: `walk_subd_limit_cross_plane(cage_mesh, plane_point, plane_normal, num_walk_samples=400)` returns `CrossCurveResult(points, face_indices_crossed, num_intersections, honest_caveat)`; samples a uniform (u,v) grid on each cage face using the Stam (1998) closed-form limit-position evaluator (`stam_limit_position` — bi-cubic B-spline for regular valence-4 patches, eigenstructure for extraordinary vertices); sign changes in signed plane distance are detected between adjacent grid samples (u-adjacent + v-adjacent separately); each crossing refined by 5 bisection iterations (positional error ≈ cell_size/32 ≈ face_size/32); honest caveats: discrete sample walk (coarse grid can miss sub-cell features), 5-iter bisection (not sub-pixel), boundary edge duplicates possible, extraordinary vertices use Stam eigenstructure approximation; LLM tool `subd_walk_limit_cross_plane`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (cube XY/XZ/diagonal cuts, parallel planes → empty, flat patch, grid cage, extraordinary vertex cage, degenerate cage, non-unit normal, sample-count monotonicity) — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_walk_cross_curve.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH §3–4; Schaefer-Warren (2004).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-ALONG-EDGES** ✅ — sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface curve corresponding to a chain of cage edges: `walk_along_cage_edges(cage, vertex_sequence, samples_per_edge=8)` returns `SubDEdgeWalk(points, arc_length)`; boundary edges → limit = cage (crease rule); creased interior edges → limit on sharp crease curve; smooth interior edges → smooth arc through CC limit positions; intermediate points via index-tracked CC subdivision (k = ceil(log2(spe)) levels, max 6) + per-vertex limit stencil; honest ValueError for non-adjacent vertices or out-of-range indices; LLM tool `subd_walk_edge_chain`; 14 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_walk.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-RING-FROM-EDGE** ✅ — edge ring traversal on Catmull-Clark quad cages: `compute_edge_ring(cage, start_edge)` returns `EdgeRingResult(edge_indices, is_closed, is_degenerate, transition_face_indices)`; follows opposite edges across each quad face (Maya/Blender Bridge pattern); closed on cube (4-ring) and torus (ring length = opposite-axis count); open at mesh boundary; honest degenerate flag at non-quad faces; start_edge accepts `(v0, v1)` pair or integer edge index; LLM tool `subd_compute_edge_ring`; 25 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_ring.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-LOOP-SELECT** ✅ — directional edge-loop walk on a quad cage mesh: `select_edge_loop(cage_mesh, start_edge_idx, max_steps=1000)` returns `EdgeLoopResult(edge_indices, vertex_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_vertex_valences, honest_caveat)`; walks the opposite-edge chain (Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni 2013 §3.2 'skip-2' rule): at each step crosses the current quad face to its opposite edge; terminates at irregular vertex (valence≠4), boundary edge, non-quad face, or loop closure; oracles: 4×4 torus (all valence-4) → closed loops length 4; 6×8 torus → lengths {6, 8}; cube (all valence-3) → terminates at first irregular vertex, valence=3 reported; cylinder axial-interior edge → closed ring length nu; mixed tri/quad → terminates; ValueError on out-of-range start_edge_idx; honest caveats: quads only, no tris; assumes manifold mesh; boundary vertices treated as irregular; traversal direction fixed by first adjacent face winding; LLM tool `subd_select_edge_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 25 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F §3.2; Lévy-Liu (2010) SIGGRAPH §4.

**SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** ✅ — walk a face loop on a quad cage mesh by hopping through opposite-edge adjacent quads: `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0, max_steps=1000)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; dual of the edge-loop walk — tracks faces rather than edges, useful for ring-cut planning and subdivision sweep selection; `walk_direction` 0/1 selects which opposite-edge pair to traverse: dir=0 crosses (v0,v1)↔(v2,v3) edges, dir=1 crosses (v1,v2)↔(v3,v0) edges; on a regular torus the two directions produce orthogonal face rings; terminates at non-quad face, boundary edge, or loop closure; oracles: 4×4 torus dir=0 → closed ring length 4; 4×6 torus dir=0→length 4, dir=1→length 6; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 → circumferential closed ring length 12; cube → closed 4-ring; mixed tri/quad → terminated; single-quad cage → terminated; non-quad start face → immediate termination; ValueError on out-of-range start_face_idx or walk_direction not in {0,1}; honest caveats: quads only — non-quad face terminates immediately; boundary edges terminate walk; walk_direction relative to start face winding; one-directional (no back-propagation); manifold mesh assumed; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F §3.2; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes §3.2.

**SUBD-CAGE-SUBDIVIDE-EDGE** ✅ — localized single-edge refinement on a SubD control cage (not a full Catmull-Clark pass): `subdivide_edge(cage, edge_index, position_t=0.5, split_strategy='quad') -> SubdivideEdgeResult`; inserts midpoint vertex v_m = lerp(v_a, v_b, t) on the target edge; each of the 1–2 adjacent faces split into face_a [p0, v_m, p_{n-1}] (triangle) + face_b [v_m, p1, ..., p_{n-1}] (quad for n=4); cube oracle: V=8→9, F=6→8, E=12→15, Euler 9−15+8=2 ✓; boundary-edge split: 1 adjacent face only; invalid edge_index → ValueError; position_t clamp [1e-9, 1−1e-9]; honest flag `has_non_quad_input` for non-quad input faces; sharpness/bevel-weight not preserved across edge-index remapping; LLM tool `subd_subdivide_edge`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 24 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_subdivide_edge.py`. Ref: Catmull & Clark 1978; Stam 1998 §4 local refinement; Maya polySplit API.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** ✅ — collapse a quad cage edge to a single vertex: `collapse_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx) -> EdgeCollapseResult`; merges v_a and v_b into their midpoint v_m = (v_a + v_b) / 2; all face index references to v_a or v_b are rewritten to v_m; faces that contained both endpoints become degenerate (repeated vertex) and are removed; vertex list is compacted (net -1 vertex per collapse); cube oracle: collapse top-front edge (4,5) → 7 verts, 2 degenerate faces removed; cylinder: axial edge collapse reduces vertex count by 1; plane: interior shared edge → both vertex and face count shrink; midpoint position oracle ✓; all face indices valid post-collapse ✓; invalid edge_idx → ValueError; honest caveats: midpoint-only (no QEM / Garland-Heckbert 1997 cost-driven placement); CC limit surface shape changes; crease annotations on incident edges not preserved; vertex/face indices invalidated after collapse; LLM tool `subd_collapse_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 14 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes §3.2; Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F §4.

**SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** ✅ — merge a list of N cage vertices (by index) into their centroid, updating all adjacent face indices and removing degenerate faces: `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices) -> VertexMergeResult`; computes v_c = mean of all named vertex positions; replaces every face reference to any named vertex with v_c; faces containing ≥ 2 named vertices become degenerate (repeated vertex) and are removed; vertex list compacted (net -(|S|-1) vertices); special cases: empty or single-vertex list → no-op; duplicate indices → deduplicated; non-adjacent vertices (no shared edge) → no faces removed, vertex count drops by |S|-1; cube oracle: merge all 4 corners of isolated quad → 3 verts removed, 1 face removed, 0 faces survive; 2-vertex merge on plane → equivalent to edge_collapse (same vertex count, same faces removed, centroid=midpoint); 3-vertex centroid oracle ✓; all face indices valid post-merge ✓; out-of-range index → ValueError; honest caveats: centroid placement only — NO quadric error metric (Garland-Heckbert 1997 §3); CC limit surface shape changes; crease annotations on incident edges not preserved; vertex/face indices invalidated after merge; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes §3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM §3.

**SUBD-LIMIT-CRITICAL-POINTS** ✅ — discrete Morse critical points (∇f = 0) on Catmull-Clark SubD limit surfaces: `find_critical_points(cage, scalar_field, sample_density=4) -> CriticalPointsReport`; classifies interior vertices using lower/upper link under Simulation-of-Simplicity total order (Edelsbrunner-Mücke 1990) — minima (Lk⁻ empty), maxima (Lk⁺ empty), saddles (#components(Lk⁻) + #components(Lk⁺) > 2); Morse-Euler verification #max − #sad + #min = χ(V−E+F); scalar fields: height_z/height_x/height_y/radius; oracle depth bar: sphere from cube cage → 1 max + 1 min + 0 sad (χ=2, Euler passes); torus (axis along Y, Morse generic) → 1 max + 1 min + 2 sad (χ=0); flat/tilted-plane open mesh → 0 critical points; honest caveat: Bott-Samelson degenerate fields (axis-symmetric height on upright torus) not handled — euler_check flags violations; LLM tool `subd_find_critical_points`; 16 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_critical_points.py` (Edelsbrunner-Harer 2010 §1).

**BREP-SHELL-WALL-CHECK** ✅ — post-shell wall-thickness verification against manufacturing process requirements: `check_shell_walls(body, process, material) -> ShellWallReport`; injection moulding spec from Menges 2001 §3.3 Table 3.3 (t_min/t_max per material, flow-length correction +0.5 mm/100 mm); sheet metal from Boothroyd-Dewhurst §5 (constant-wall + §5.4 bend-radius multiplier); FDM/SLA/SLS/DLP/MJF nozzle-diameter minimum wall; per-face `FaceWallResult` with violation text; `violations_thin`/`violations_thick` lists; honest caveat: static rule-based only, no CFD or mould-fill simulation; LLM tool `brep_check_shell_walls`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (2mm ABS → pass; 0.5mm ABS → thin; 0.5mm FDM → pass; 0.2mm FDM → thin; 6mm ABS → thick; Menges Table 3.3 oracle for PP/PC/LCP/PVC/POM/PEEK; flow-length correction; sheet-metal Al; SLA; nozzle override) — `kerf-cad-core/geom/shell_wall_check.py`.

### Core platform

- **Auth + projects + files + chat (CRUD)** ✅ — Postgres, JWT, Google OAuth.
- **Plugin monorepo (`packages/kerf-*`)** ✅ — `kerf-core` app factory + entry-point loader; ~25 plugin packages; 864+ tests.
- **Single-binary build + brew/curl install** ✅ — embedded Vite SPA (~32 MB).
- **Auth-optional local mode** ✅ — `POST /auth/bootstrap-local` singleton user.
- **Cloud: workshop sharing, billing, LLM pricing, free/paid buckets + wallet** ✅ — USD-display, credits at cost, BYO-key plumbing.
- **Cloud: git (commits/branches/merge/GitHub sync) + git Storer** ✅.
- **Large-file git handling** ✅ — pointer kind, Phase 1.
- **Diff-based + compressed revisions** ✅ — 82× shrink.
- **Workspaces (orgs), activity timeline, avatars/CDN, collapsible chat** ✅.
- **E2E Playwright + per-plugin pytest suites** ✅.
- **Billing-ledger schema on fresh databases** ✅.

### Scripting / SDK

- **`.script.py` via `kerf-sdk`** ✅ — `/v1/rpc` JSON-RPC over the LLM tool registry; API tokens; PyPI publish.
- **SDKs: Python · TypeScript · Rust · Go · Lua** ✅ — same `/v1/rpc` wire format.

### Parametric core

- **Equations / global parameters** ✅ — `.equations`, mathjs.
- **Configurations / variants** ✅ — per-file param overrides, BOM rollup.
- **Materials database** ✅ — `.material` kind, 200 seeded materials.
- **Two coexisting kernels** ✅ — `.jscad` (mesh) + `.feature` (OCCT BRep), shared `.sketch`/`.assembly`/`.drawing`.
- **Pure-Python B-rep + NURBS kernel** ✅ — validated `Body` topology, tolerant booleans, G1/G2 fillets, closest-point, hardened SSI, parametric history DAG with persistent face naming. 620 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests.

### Geometry kernel — depth

The pure-Python kernel (`packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/`) now matches Rhino/Blender-class construction depth with an analytic foundation:

| Module | Description | Status |
|---|---|---|
| **`brep.py`** | B-rep topology: radial-edge `Body→Solid→Shell→Face→Loop→Coedge→Edge→Vertex`, nine Euler operators, Euler–Poincaré invariant enforced | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/topology_euler_check.py`** | **BREP-TOPOLOGY-EULER-CHECK**: full generalised Euler-Poincaré verifier V-E+F = 2(S-G)+H (Mantyla 1988 §6; Hoffmann 1989 §5); `verify_euler_topology(Body)` + `verify_euler_topology_from_dict(faces, ...)` + `EulerCheckReport` dataclass; union-find shell count; oracle helpers for cube/torus/disjoint cubes; LLM tool `brep_verify_euler_topology`; 16 hermetic tests (cube χ=2, torus χ=0, disjoint cubes S=2/χ=4, inner loops, violation flags). Pure-Python. CAVEATS: genus/inner-loops require caller hints in dict mode; vertex dedup after sew/heal may cause spurious failure (degenerate_vertices_hint flag). | ✅ shipped |
| **`brep_build.py`** | Analytic verbs (box/cylinder/sphere/Coons patch) → `validate_body`-clean `Body` | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 §3 + Mantyla 1988 §6); counts dangling / boundary / manifold / non-manifold edges; isolated vertices; degenerate (zero-length) edges; union-find shell connectivity components; Euler–Poincaré V-E+F residual; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold`; 11 hermetic oracle tests (closed cube → manifold=12/boundary=0/components=1; open box → boundary=4/manifold=8; T-shape → nonmanifold≥1; two disconnected cubes → components=2). Pure-Python, no OCCT. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 §3 + Mantyla 1988 §6); manifold/boundary/nonmanifold/dangling counts; isolated vertices; degenerate edges; union-find shell components; Euler–Poincaré V-E+F; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold` | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/vertex_degree_check.py`** | **BREP-VERTEX-DEGREE-CHECK**: count incident edges per vertex; flag boundary (degree < expected_degree) and non-manifold (degree > expected_degree + 2); `VertexDegreeReport` dataclass with `num_vertices`, `degree_histogram` (dict[int,int]), `num_boundary_vertices`, `num_non_manifold_vertices`, `max_degree`, `irregular_vertex_indices`, `honest_caveat`; `check_vertex_degrees(brep_or_mesh, expected_degree=4)`; oracle helpers for cube + tetrahedron; LLM tool `brep_check_vertex_degrees`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests. Pure-Python. CAVEATS: edge-based degree only — does NOT analyse face-fan angular order or non-manifold edges at high-degree vertices. Refs: Mantyla 1988 §3.4; Hoffmann 1989 §4. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_edge_metrics.py`** | **BREP-SUM-EDGE-LENGTHS**: total edge length + kind/curve-type breakdowns for cutting-cost estimation; `total_edge_length` / `edge_length_by_kind` / `edges_by_curve_type` / `compute_edge_metrics`; linear→Euclidean, circular→radius×angle, freeform→adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre (Stoer-Bulirsch §3 + Piegl-Tiller §5.4); oracles: 100×50 rect=300, unit cube=12, sphere 12 great-circle r=50=3769.91; LLM tools `brep_total_edge_length` + `brep_edge_length_by_kind`; 20 hermetic tests | ✅ shipped |
| **`boolean.py`** | Tolerant pure-Python solid booleans (regularised cut/fuse/common) over the primitive matrix, 2-manifold result | ✅ shipped |
| **`fillet_solid.py` / `chamfer.py`** | G1/G2 surface blend + edge fillet + variable chamfer | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/auto_chamfer.py`** | Auto-chamfer recommendation (ISO 13715): dihedral-angle classification → safety / manufacturing / cosmetic / no-chamfer; `brep_recommend_chamfers` + `brep_apply_chamfer_recommendations` LLM tools | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/auto_fillet.py`** | Auto-fillet recommendation engine (Peterson 1974 + Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002) — classifies interior/exterior corners, sizes radii per design intent, estimates Kt reduction; LLM tools `brep_recommend_fillets` + `brep_apply_fillet_recommendations` | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | BREP-FILLET-RECOMMEND-RADIUS — per-edge radius recommendation combining 4 criteria: (1) face-size cap r≤face_min/4 (Boothroyd-Dewhurst §4), (2) Peterson 1974 §2.3 notch Kt formula r=0.1×notch_depth (tension+bending, analytic only, NOT FEA), (3) material stress-relief floor r≥factor×wall_thickness (steel 0.05, cast_iron 0.08, etc.), (4) tool constraint r≥tool_radius_mm + sharp-edge preservation; `RadiusRecommendation` dataclass with criteria_radii transparency dict; LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius`; 21 hermetic oracle tests | ✅ shipped |
| **`fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | Per-edge fillet radius recommendation (Peterson 1974 §2.3; Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002 §4) — LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius` | ✅ shipped |
| **`chamfer_recommend_size.py`** | Per-edge chamfer size recommendation (Drozda-Wick §3-7; DIN 74:1974 Form A/B; ISO 13715:2017 §5) — deburring 0.5mm×45°; countersink; cosmetic; manufacturing — LLM tool `brep_recommend_chamfer_size` | ✅ shipped |
| **`offset.py`** | Exact-distance surface/curve/loop offsets with self-intersection trim | ✅ shipped |
| **`surface_offset.py`** | NURBS surface offset (Tiller-Hanson 1984 + Hoschek 1988): CP face-normal displacement, iterative isotropic-error refinement, Möller 1997 self-intersection detection, local-loop trim; `nurbs_surface_offset` LLM tool; 4 analytical oracle tests (plane/cylinder/sphere/C-shape) | ✅ shipped |
| **`curve_offset_2d.py`** | NURBS 2D curve offset + self-intersection trim (Tiller-Hanson 1984) — foundation for flat patterns, CAM toolpath offset, hatch fill | ✅ shipped |
| **`coons.py`** | Boundary-interpolation Coons patches, exact to 1e-12 | ✅ shipped |
| **`network_surface.py`** | N-sided patch: N=3 Hosaka-Kimura triangular Coons, N=4 Gregory twist-corrected Coons, N≥5 Wachspress polygon blend; `fairness_metric` bending energy; LLM tool `nurbs_n_sided_patch` | ✅ shipped |
| **`inversion.py`** | Closest-point / point-inversion (Piegl 6.1, analytic partials on rational surfaces) | ✅ shipped |
| **`curve_projection.py`** | Point→curve / point→surface projection (Newton-Raphson + arc-length fallback, Hu-Wallner 2006); `ProjectionResult` dataclass; `distance_curve_to_curve`; LLM tool `nurbs_project_point` | ✅ shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations; **NURBS-CURVE-SELF-INTERSECT enhanced** — `curve_self_intersect_robust`: Piegl-Tiller §5.5 AABB-tree recursive subdivision + Sederberg 1985 bisection stop criterion + Newton–Raphson on \|C(t1)−C(t2)\|²; figure-8 Bézier oracle verified ≤1e-9; 33 new tests green; honest-flag: multiplicity-3 intersections not detected | ✅ shipped |
| **`intersection_degen.py` — Degenerate SSI (Legendre canonical forms)** | `detect_degenerate_ssi` + `compute_degenerate_ssi_curve` + `ssi_extended`; handles coaxial cylinders, coplanar planes, sphere-tangent-plane, Legendre/Weierstrass conic section for tangent quadric pairs; LLM tool `nurbs_ssi_with_degenerate_check` registered; 27 hermetic tests with analytical oracles | ✅ shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations | ✅ shipped |
| **`edge_curve_from_face_pair.py`** | B-rep edge-curve extraction: SSI → longest branch → degree-3 NURBS fit + UV traces on both faces (Sederberg-Parry 1986 / Patrikalakis-Maekawa §7); LLM tool `brep_extract_edge_curve_from_faces` | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/edge_curve_extend.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CURVE-EXTEND**: extend a B-rep edge's underlying NurbsCurve beyond its parametric domain by ΔL mm, preserving G1 (tangent) continuity at the join (Piegl & Tiller §10.4 tangent extrapolation; Mortenson §3.7). `extend_edge_curve(curve, delta_length_mm, end, continuity)` → `EdgeExtendResult(extended_curve, original_length_mm, extended_length_mm, end_continuity_achieved, honest_caveat)`. Method: cubic Bézier control points colinear with end tangent; degree-1 originals raised to degree-3. LLM tool `brep_extend_edge_curve` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 21 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: G1 only — G2 curvature-continuous extension not yet implemented; extension segment is a straight line (curvature at join drops to zero); acceptable for trim-surface / edge-healing use-cases. Refs: Piegl & Tiller §10.4; Mortenson §3.7. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/edge_chamfer_variable.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CHAMFER-VARIABLE**: variable-width chamfer strip along a 2D edge curve for ergonomic edge treatments (handle bevels with grip-width variations). Width ramps linearly from `width_start_mm` (t=0) to `width_end_mm` (t=1) via `w(t) = w_start + t*(w_end-w_start)`; both sides offset perpendicularly by `w(t)/2`. `ChamferVariableSpec` / `ChamferVariableResult` dataclasses; `generate_variable_chamfer(spec)` entry point. LLM tool `brep_generate_variable_chamfer` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 27 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: input is a 2D polyline only — 3D space-curve chamfer that modifies B-rep solid topology is not yet supported (requires generalising `chamfer.py` topology surgery to curved edges, P2/P3 scope). Strip points are a sampled polyline approximation, not an exact NURBS offset curve. Refs: Piegl & Tiller §10.5 (Variable offsets); Mortenson §9.3 (Edge blends). | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/history/`** | Parametric history DAG + `feature_id::role::fingerprint` persistent naming — downstream fillet survives upstream parameter edits | ✅ shipped |
| **G3 surfacing** | `feature_blend_srf_g3` (surfacing.py:1376) + `feature_g3_chain_blend` (surfacing.py:1894) registered LLM tools; `blend_srf_g3` / `curvature_rate_continuity_residual` / `zebra_stripe` / `reflection_lines` / `curvature_comb` exported from `geom/__init__.py`; `feature_zebra_analysis` + `feature_isophote_analysis` wired | ✅ shipped |
| **General solid boolean** | NURBS-faced / non-axis-aligned solids; classification-first B-rep pipeline (SSI seeds → whole-face classify → sew); analytic fast-paths for box/sphere/cylinder; LLM tool registered (`nurbs_solid_boolean`); 18 hermetic tests — sphere∩box, Steinmetz, freeform NURBS, self-intersection guard | ✅ shipped |
| **General solid boolean** | NURBS×NURBS solid boolean with exact UV-trim at SSI curves (GK-P-B); whole-face fallback retained for tangential cases; 22 hermetic tests green | ✅ shipped |
| **Body-body imprint with edge tagging** | `imprint_body(target, tool, mode)` in `geom/imprint.py`: projects all tool edges onto target faces via `imprint_curve_on_face`, tags new edges with `ImprintTag(source_body_id, source_edge_id)`. `mode='intersect'` AABB+plane proximity filter; `mode='all'` for design-intent transfer. LLM tool `brep_imprint_body` registered in plugin. 4 oracle tests (box-on-box footprint, provenance coverage, no-intersect no-op, mode comparison). | ✅ shipped |
| **Surface fairing + Sapidis curve fairing** | `surface_fairing.py`: `fair_surface()` (iterative discrete-Laplacian control-net smoothing, 3 boundary modes) + `fair_surface_bend()` (sparse bending-energy linear solve via scipy.sparse); `curve_toolkit.py`: `fair_curve(sapidis=True)` (Sapidis & Farin 1994 iterative knot removal + insertion); LLM tools `surface_fair` + `curve_fair` registered; 19 hermetic tests (σ(z) oracle, boundary preservation, energy-monotone, Sapidis curvature-variance reduction) | ✅ shipped |
| **Variable-radius G2 fillet (Stadler 2006)** | `variable_radius_fillet_g2` + `fillet_radius_field_planner` in `geom/surface_fillet.py`; `nurbs_fillet_variable_g2` LLM tool registered; G2 continuity along radius gradient via cubic Hermite curvature blending; 48 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests | ✅ shipped |
| **GK-P: Variable-section edge blend (Vida-Martin-Varady 1994)** | `edge_blend.py` — `CrossSection` (rect/circle/ellipse/polygon), `variable_section_blend` (linear / cubic_hermite / C2 methods), `morph_cross_sections` (Bezier corner rounding per Hartmann 1998); `nurbs_edge_blend_variable_section` LLM tool registered; exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 37 tests, 4 analytical oracles (volume, rect→circle morph, C1 continuity, volume monotonic) | ✅ shipped |
| **Post-Boolean continuity recovery (G1/G2 seam blending)** | `recover_continuity_at_seam` / `recover_continuity_body` in `geom/continuity_recovery.py`; degree-3 Hermite blend strip inserted at G0-only seams; G1 tangent < 5° + G2 curvature-rate residual oracle; `brep_recover_continuity` LLM tool; 29 hermetic tests green. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/wall_thickness.py`** | Wall-thickness analysis with material guidelines — `analyze_wall_thickness` (SDF-ray-cast, Stroud-Nagy §17.2), `material_thickness_guideline` (ABS/PP/PE/PC/Nylon/PVC/…), `flag_thin_walls`; LLM tools `brep_analyze_wall_thickness` + `brep_check_moldability` ✅ | ✅ shipped |
| **GK-P: Mold parting surface construction (Yu-Fan 2003)** | `mold_parting_surface.py`: `construct_parting_surface` (radial ruled quads from parting line to mold bbox), `construct_with_shutoff_inserts` (undercut shutoff patches), `validate_parting_surface`; LLM tool `brep_construct_parting_surface` registered in `kerf-mold`; 22 hermetic oracle tests pass | ✅ shipped |
| **GK-P Curvature-comb peaks + variance metrics (Farin 1990)** | `curvature_comb_peaks` (peak detection, sharpness), `curvature_variance_metric` (variance/std/skewness/kurtosis/total variation), `isophote_density_metric` (Pottmann-Wallner 2001 Ch 10); `continuity_audit(include_curvature_metrics=True)`; LLM tool `nurbs_curvature_metrics` registered; 16 tests green | ✅ shipped |
| **GK-P: Exact arc-length-preserving offset** | `exact_length_offset.py` — Klass 1980 / Maekawa 1999 §3: Tiller-Hanson initial offset + secant iteration on displacement scale; `offset_curve_arclength_preserving` / `exact_arclength_match_error` / `compare_offsets`; LLM tool `nurbs_offset_arclength_preserving`; 11 hermetic analytic-oracle tests | ✅ shipped |
| **GK-P: Quadratic → cubic NURBS elevation** | Piegl-Tiller §5.5 specialisation (Lyche-Mørken 1988): exact degree-2 → degree-3 B-spline promotion with shape preservation; per-segment closed-form (`Q1=P0/3+2/3·P1`, `Q2=2/3·P1+P2/3`); rational/weighted support; surface per-direction; `auto_elevate_to_degree_3` body normalizer for STEP import; `nurbs_elevate_to_cubic` LLM tool registered — `geom/degree_2_to_3.py` | ✅ shipped |

| **`geom/face_centroid.py`** | **BREP-FACE-AREA-WEIGHTED-CENTROID**: area-weighted surface centroid of a B-rep shell/solid; `face_area` / `face_centroid` / `surface_centroid`; Gauss-Legendre 16×16 per face; supports Plane/Cylinder/Sphere/Torus/NurbsSurface; LLM tool `brep_surface_centroid`; oracles: unit cube area=6/centroid=(0.5,0.5,0.5), unit sphere area=4π/centroid=(0,0,0); 15 hermetic tests. CAVEAT: trimmed faces (inner loops) use bounding-box UV domain — v1 heuristic. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/iso_curve_extract.py`** | **NURBS-EXTRACT-ISO-CURVES-AT-PARAM**: Piegl-Tiller §5.3 knot-insertion iso-curve extraction — `extract_iso_curve_u(srf, u)`, `extract_iso_curve_v(srf, v)`, `extract_iso_grid(srf, nu, nv)`; rational (homogeneous-coords) + non-rational; LLM tools `nurbs_extract_iso_u` + `nurbs_extract_iso_v`; 24 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (bilinear round-trip 1e-12, Bezier degree/knot-vector check, sphere octant radius variance < 1e-9, cylinder closure, boundary CPs, grid counts). | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/face_neighbor_walk.py`** | **BREP-FACE-NEIGHBOR-WALK**: face-adjacency traversal for CNC tool-path routing, geodesic shortest-path between faces, paint-area planning; `face_adjacency_graph` (inverted edge→faces index, O(F·E_avg)), `face_neighbors`, `bfs_from_face(depth_cap=10)`, `shortest_face_path` (BFS, discrete hop-count geodesic), `FaceAdjacencyGraph` dataclass with `connected_components`; LLM tools `brep_face_neighbors` + `brep_shortest_face_path`; oracles: unit cube each face=4 neighbours, BFS depth-2 reaches opposite face, opposite-face path=2 hops; open cylinder side=2/cap=1 neighbour; two disconnected cubes=2 components; 41 hermetic tests. CAVEAT: adjacency is edge-sharing only — vertex-only (point-touching) contact is NOT adjacent (Weiler 1985 §3 radial-edge model). | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/face_planarity.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PLANARITY-CHECK**: determine if a B-rep face is planar within tolerance; fit best-fit plane via SVD on uniform samples×samples UV grid (Pratt 1987 §3; Eberly §6.6 orthogonal regression); returns `PlanarityReport` (is_planar, plane_origin, plane_normal, max_deviation, planarity_score); default tolerance = 1e-4 × bbox diagonal; `check_face_planarity` pure-Python API; LLM tool `brep_check_face_planarity`; oracles: planar NURBS max_dev<1e-9, sphere octant is_planar=False with expected curvature depth, thin 1° arc boundary case, tilted plane, analytic Plane/Sphere surfaces; 12 hermetic tests. CAVEAT (v1): full UV-domain sampling — inner trim loops (holes) are NOT excluded; plane fit may be slightly biased for faces with large inner voids. Useful for: sheet-metal flat-pattern feasibility, simple-face fast-rendering, planar-face cooling-channel routing. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/face_developable_check.py`** | **BREP-FACE-DEVELOPABLE-CHECK**: verify if a B-rep face is developable (can be unrolled flat without stretching). A surface is developable iff Gaussian curvature K = κ_1·κ_2 = 0 everywhere (do Carmo §3.6; Pottmann-Wallner §4). Algorithm: sample N×N UV grid, compute K via shape operator at each point using `normal_curvature_at`, test max|K| < tolerance; also reports mean|K|, valid sample count, and ruled direction (kappa_1 or kappa_2 identically zero). `DevelopabilityReport` dataclass; `check_face_developable(face, tolerance=1e-3, samples=10)`; LLM tool `brep_check_face_developable`. Depth-bar: cylinder K=0→developable=True; sphere K=1/R²→False; cone K=0 on rulings→True; torus K varies sign→False; plane K=0→True. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 24 hermetic tests green. HONEST: sampling-based — max|K| is a lower bound on true supremum; high-curvature pockets between grid points may be missed; use samples≥20 for production confidence. Useful for: sheet-metal flat-pattern feasibility, ruled-surface validation. | ✅ shipped |
| **BREP half-space volume** | Given a B-rep solid + cutting plane (point + normal), compute volume on each side via divergence theorem (Mortenson §11.6). Plane faces: Green's theorem + Sutherland-Hodgman clip. Curved faces: GL quadrature on UV sub-quads. LLM tool `brep_volume_above_plane`. Depth-bar: unit cube z=0.5 → 0.5/0.5; unit sphere equator → each half 4π/6 ≈ 2.094; cylinder r=1 h=2 x=0 → each half π. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/face_compatible_resplit.py`** | **BREP-FACE-COMPATIBLE-RESPLIT**: given two adjacent NURBS faces sharing an edge but with incompatible UV parameterisations, insert knots into both so the shared edge has compatible parameter spans — prerequisite for surface sewing, BREP repair, and Boolean operations. `make_faces_compatible(face_a, face_b) → CompatibilityResult` (face_a_new, face_b_new, knots_inserted, shared_edge_dir_a/b, degree_mismatch, already_compatible). Algorithm: compute union of internal breakpoints (P&T §6.5); insert missing knots via tensor-product Boehm Algorithm A5.1; auto-detect shared boundary by geometric proximity of iso-parameter mid-points. Depth-bar: face_a=[0,0,0,0.5,1,1,1] + face_b=[0,0,0,0.3,0.7,1,1,1] → both [0,0,0,0.3,0.5,0.7,1,1,1] after compatibilization. LLM tool `brep_make_faces_compatible` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 14 hermetic tests green. HONEST: degree mismatch requires degree elevation (Hoffmann §6) — flagged via `degree_mismatch=True`, not auto-applied; rational NURBS weight-correct; multiplicity>1 not forced. (Piegl-Tiller §6.5 + Hoffmann 1989 §6) | ✅ shipped |
| **`surface_area_exact.py`** | Exact NURBS surface area via first-fundamental-form integrand A = ∫∫ sqrt(EG−F²) du dv (do Carmo §2.5 / Mortenson §10.4); 5×5 Gauss-Legendre per knot-span cell + adaptive subdivision; `SurfaceAreaReport`; LLM tool `nurbs_surface_area_exact`; 18 analytic-oracle tests (unit plane 1e-12, sphere zone <1%, cylinder+torus domain oracles). Honest: full UV domain only in v1 — trimming not supported. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/face_area_exact.py`** | **BREP-FACE-AREA-EXACT**: compute the exact area of a B-rep Face whose underlying surface is a NurbsSurface, using the first fundamental form A = ∫∫ sqrt(EG−F²) du dv (do Carmo §2.5; Piegl & Tiller §10.3; Farin §11.2). Reuses `compute_exact_surface_area` (5×5 GL per knot-span cell) for the NurbsSurface fast path; generic path uses N×N GL per cell with adaptive subdivision (default: `gauss_order=8`, `adaptive_subdivisions=4`). `FaceAreaResult` dataclass: `area_mm2`, `num_quadrature_points`, `relative_error_estimate`, `honest_caveat`. Also handles analytic surfaces (Plane/Cylinder/Sphere/Torus) via finite-difference partials. LLM tool `brep_compute_face_area_exact` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 34 hermetic tests green (NurbsSurface flat 10×10→100mm² within 1e-9; sphere R=1→4π within 0.01%; sphere R=2→16π within 0.01%; cylinder R=2 h=5→62.83 within 0.01%; torus R=2 r=0.5→39.48 within 0.1%; FaceAreaResult contract; trim-caveat; gauss_order consistency; re-export). HONEST: trimmed faces (faces with inner loops) use bounding-rectangle approximation — trim curves NOT honoured in v1; `honest_caveat` field explicitly reports this. Polynomial NURBS approximations of curved surfaces (cylinder, torus) under-report area by the chord error of the spline (~2–8%) compared to the exact analytic surface. | ✅ shipped |
| **`geom/principal_curvature_viz.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PRINCIPAL-CURVATURE-VIZ**: sample κ₁, κ₂ (principal curvatures) over a B-rep Face on a U×V grid + SVG/PNG false-colour heatmap. `PrincipalCurvatureSample` dataclass (u, v, kappa_1, kappa_2, gauss_K, mean_H, is_degenerate); `PrincipalCurvatureVizResult` (samples list, svg_heatmap str, png_bytes bytes\|None, honest_caveat str); `sample_principal_curvatures(face, nu=20, nv=20, export_svg=True, export_png=False)`. Algorithm: exact analytic derivatives via `surface_derivatives` (Piegl-Tiller Alg. A3.6) for NurbsSurface; finite-difference fallback for other surfaces with `evaluate(u,v)`. Shape-operator characteristic equation (do Carmo §3.4): κ₁ = H + √(H²−K), κ₂ = H − √(H²−K); K = (LN−M²)/(EG−F²); H = (EN−2FM+GL)/(2(EG−F²)). SVG heatmap: viridis false-colour of |κ₁| per UV cell; PNG via pure-Python encoder (no Pillow). LLM tool `brep_face_principal_curvature_viz`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 33 hermetic tests green (plane κ=0 exact; exact rational sphere |κ|=1/R ±5e-3; exact rational cylinder |κ₂|=1/R ±1e-3; torus K sign-change; SVG/PNG validity; K=κ₁·κ₂ identity; H=(κ₁+κ₂)/2 identity; grid clamping). HONEST: uniform UV-parameter grid only — high-curvature pockets between grid points are missed (lower bound on max|κ|); not adaptive; polar/degenerate points (|S_u×S_v|<1e-14) set is_degenerate=True with NaN curvatures; heatmap maps |κ₁|, not signed κ₁. Refs: do Carmo §3.4; Mortenson §6.5; Pottmann-Wallner §4. | ✅ shipped |

**GK-P50: NURBS arc-length inversion** ✅ — `invert_arc_length` (Newton–Raphson + bisection fall-back; Piegl & Tiller §11.2 + Sederberg CAGD §6.4). Returns `ArcLengthInvertResult{t_param, residual_mm, iterations, honest_caveat}`. Used for chord-length parameterisation, even-spaced CAM toolpaths, rebar layout. Wired as `nurbs_invert_arc_length` LLM tool. 19 tests green. Caveat: highly non-uniform knot vectors may trigger bisection fall-back (still converges, just slower).

- **SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** ✅ — `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; face-dual of edge-loop walk: hops through opposite-edge adjacent quads; walk_direction 0/1 gives orthogonal rings on regular tori; 4×6 torus dir=0→ring 4, dir=1→ring 6; cube → closed 4-ring; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 → closed ring 12; mixed tri/quad → terminated; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; honest: quads only — non-quad terminates; 20 tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) §3.2; Hoppe (1996) §3.2.
- **SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** ✅ — `collapse_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx)` merges endpoints v_a + v_b → midpoint v_m; degenerate faces removed; midpoint position oracle ✓; cube → 7 verts, 2 faces removed; all face indices valid post-collapse; invalid edge_idx → ValueError; LLM tool `subd_collapse_edge`; honest: midpoint only — no QEM; 14 tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) §3.2; Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) §4.
- **SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** ✅ — `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices)` merges N cage vertices into centroid v_c; degenerate faces removed; 2-vertex merge ≡ edge collapse; 4-corner merge on isolated quad collapses it entirely; non-adjacent merge → no faces removed; empty/single list → no-op; duplicates deduplicated; 3-vertex centroid oracle ✓; all face indices valid; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; honest: centroid only — no QEM (Garland-Heckbert 1997); 20 tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) §3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) §3.
- **SUBD-CAGE-DUAL-MESH** ✅ — `compute_dual_mesh(cage_mesh)` returns `DualMeshResult(dual_vertices, dual_faces, num_irregular_dual_faces, honest_caveat)`; dual vertices = one face centroid per primal face; dual faces = CCW-ordered ring of neighboring face centroids per primal vertex (atan2 angular sort on tangent plane); cube oracle: 8 verts + 6 quads → 6 dual verts + 8 triangular dual faces (combinatorial octahedron), 0 irregular; 4×4 torus (all valence-4) → 16 dual verts + 16 quad dual faces, 0 irregular; 2×2 plane grid → 4 dual verts + 9 dual faces, boundary vertices counted irregular; cylinder barrel (open) → correct dual vertex/face count, boundary rings flagged irregular; all dual face indices valid; LLM tool `subd_compute_dual_mesh`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 28 oracle-asserted tests — `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/dual_mesh.py`. HONEST: closed manifold meshes only for complete dual faces — boundary primal edges produce INCOMPLETE (open) dual faces; angular sort (atan2) works on convex vertex stars but may mis-order concave or nearly co-planar stars; dual vertices are primal face centroids, NOT CC limit-surface points; non-manifold vertices produce topologically undefined dual faces. Refs: Bossen-Heckbert (1996) §3.1; Bommes-Lévy-Pietroni (2013) §3.2.
